		function get_aamCookie (c_name)
		{
		var i,x,y,ARRcookies=document.cookie.split(";");
		for (i=0;i<ARRcookies.length;i++)
		   {
		   x=ARRcookies[i].substr(0,ARRcookies[i].indexOf("="));
		   y=ARRcookies[i].substr(ARRcookies[i].indexOf("=")+1);
		   x=x.replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g,"");
		   if (x==c_name)
		      {
		      return unescape(y);
		      }
		   }
		}

// These 2 functions have a scoping issue, with jQuery. So they can't be included into the standard set of functions below.
function isSearchValid(inputfield, inputform) {
	var searchStr = jQuery(inputfield).val();
	if (searchStr === '') {
		jQuery(inputfield).focus();
		return false;
	}else{
		trackLink2(jQuery(inputfield)[0], searchStr, {"events": "event1"});
		return true;
	}
}
function submitSearch(searchStr) {
	jQuery('#NavR_Header_Search_Input').val(searchStr);
	jQuery('#NavR_Header_Search_Form').submit();
}
// End Search Functions.
var fullWidthMode = true; //behavior of resizing and centering. needs to be false for new gallery.

if(readCookie('rd-xfinity-comcast-eonline') === '1' || readCookie('rd-xfinity-comcast-eonline-iPad') === '1') {
	//mave xfinity header to global header section to avoid ad skin overlap
	setTimeout(function() {
		var xfinityDivs = jQuery("#page").prevAll("div");
		jQuery.each(xfinityDivs, function() {
			if (jQuery(this).find("iframe[src*='http://xfinity.comcast.net/globalnav/1']")) {
					var xfinityDiv = jQuery(this);
					jQuery(xfinityDiv).prependTo("#HHeader");
			}
		});
	},400);
}

	window.open(facebookURL, '', 'menubar=no,toolbar=no,resizable=yes,scrollbars=yes,height=500,width=750');
}

	var twitterURL = "http://twitter.com/intent/follow?screen_name="+acct;
	window.open(twitterURL,'','menubar=no,toolbar=no,resizable=yes,scrollbars=yes,height=500,width=750');
}

<script type="text/javascript" >
	//the nav content is to match the width of the main content.
	//lp_global controls that change so we listen for the notification that the main widget layout area has changed
	(function(){
		if(typeof lp_global !== "undefined"){
			lp_global.dispatcher.on("LAYOUT_CHANGED",function(event){
				if (typeof eonline_Globalnav !== 'undefined') {
					var nWidth = jQuery(lp_global.outer_div_class_select).width();
					//dont resize smaller
					if (nWidth >= 980) {
						eonline_Globalnav.setContentWidth(nWidth);
					}
				}
			});
		}
	})();

</script>

		    (function (strDate, edition) {
		        var articleDate = new Date(Date.parse(strDate));
 		        var articleLocalDateString;
		        if (!!moment){
		        	var localeMoment = moment(articleDate);
			        if (edition === 'de') {
			        	localeMoment.locale(edition);
			        	articleLocalDateString = localeMoment.format('llll');
			        } else if (edition === 'fr') {
			        	articleLocalDateString = localeMoment.format("[le] DD/MM/YYYY -  HH[h]mm"); //we prefer this
			        } else {
			        	articleLocalDateString = localeMoment.format('llll');
			        }
		        } else {
		        	articleLocalDateString = articleDate.toLocaleString();
		        }

		        var thisScript = document.currentScript || document.getElementById('thisScript');
		        thisScript.previousElementSibling.innerHTML = articleLocalDateString;
			    thisScript.setAttribute("id","");
			    
		    })('2016-02-10T12:58:00-08:00', "us");

				    			<p>Jack and Rose's <em>Titanic</em> love is stronger than ever.</p><p><strong><a href="/news/kate_winslet">Kate Winslet</a></strong> is more than hopeful that <strong><a href="/news/leonardo_dicaprio">Leonardo DiCaprio</a></strong> will finally win an Oscar for his work in <em>The Revenant</em>.</p><p>"It does really feel as though it's Leo's year and I'm just super excited for him," Winslet told E! News earlier today while promoting her new flick Triple 9. "And [there's] the sense of good will behind him, and that everyone wants it for him. You know, people in the streets. It's really really wonderful. I think it's real testament to that fact that he's such a lovely person and that people really not only admire him but also really like him and respect him .</p><p>"I feel quite proud of that, it's lovely," she said, holding back tears. "I keep getting emotional when I talk about Leo."</p><p>Too sweet.</p>

<script> 
	var edition = 'us';
	var encodedShareURL = encodeURI('http://www.eonline.com/news/738819/kate-winslet-gets-emotional-talking-about-leonardo-dicaprio-also-reveals-who-she-s-wearing-to-the-oscars');
	var imgSrc =  encodeURIComponent('http://www.eonline.com/eol_images/Entire_Site/201613/rs_600x600-160203121834-12555935_158864771149719_1832928640_n.jpg');
	var articleTitle = encodeURIComponent(jQuery(".entry_container .sub-headline").text());
	var imageTitle = encodeURIComponent("Leonardo DiCaprio, Kate Winslet, Marc Malkin Instagram");
	var imageCaption = encodeURIComponent("Leonardo DiCaprio, Kate Winslet, Marc Malkin Instagram");

	var titleJoin;
			
	function sharePinterest(){
	   	if (articleTitle.length > 1 && imageTitle.length > 1) {
			if (edition == 'de' || edition == 'it') {
				titleJoin = '%20%2D%20';
			} else if (edition == 'fr') {
				titleJoin = '%20de%20';
			} else {
				titleJoin = '%20from%20';
			}
		} else {
			titleJoin = "";
		}
		window.open('http://pinterest.com/pin/create/button/?url=' +  encodedShareURL + '&media=' + imgSrc + '&description=' + articleTitle + '%0A%0A' + imageCaption,  '', 'menubar=no,toolbar=no,resizable=yes,scrollbars=yes,height=253,width=750');
	}
	
	jQuery(".article_pinterest").click(function(){
				sharePinterest();
		});
	
</script>

				</div>
					<img src="http://www.eonline.com/eol_images/Entire_Site/201613/rs_600x600-160203121834-12555935_158864771149719_1832928640_n.jpg" border="0" width="600" height="600" title="Leonardo DiCaprio, Kate Winslet, Marc Malkin Instagram" alt="Leonardo DiCaprio, Kate Winslet, Marc Malkin Instagram"  />
					<span class="photo_credit">Instagram</span>
				</div>
			
							
			 
			
							
			
			
			
			 
			

			 
			
							
			
			
			
			
			
		
			
			
			
			
							
			
			
			
			
			
			
			 
			    
				
					
				    					
				    			<p>Meanwhile, Winslet revealed who she'll be wearing to the Oscars, where she's up for actress in a supporting role for her work in <em>Steve Jobs</em>.</p><p>"I'm working with Ralph Lauren and they're making something for me and it's lovely," she said. "It's been a really fun process actually and them including me quite a lot and my ideas, their ideas, and what works and what doesn't. It should be fun. I just want to be comfortable. I just don't want to have any zips that break. That's my whole thing, zips. I have zip fear."</p><p>But she refuses to let the fashion critics get the best of her. "You get on the carpet and all bets are off," Winslet said. "You just smile and wave, just get through it and then don't read any press. That's my trick--I don't look at any of it. I just get through it, have a glass of champagne and go home."</p><p><em>Triple 9</em> is in theaters on Feb. 26.</p>

        host = (host || "").replace(/:.*?$/,"");
        
        var src = "http://thyme.comcastnets.net/thyme/js/thyme.js";
        
        if ( /(au|www|uk|comcast)\.eonline\.com/.test( host ) ) {
            return { host : "www.eonline.com", key : "66aceeda8383f6d1900a593207e02a43", src: src};
        } else if ( /de\.eonline\.com/.test( host ) ) {
            return { host : "de.eonline.com", key : "b7fa646c0857f0189adb27e3eb68caa6", src: src};                
        } else if ( /it\.eonline\.com/.test( host ) ) {
            return { host : "it.eonline.com", key : "2447cb625efd382499a645ba1087de6b", src: src};                
        } else if ( /fr\.eonline\.com/.test( host ) ) {
            return { host : "fr.eonline.com", key : "23427b05a25dc9431f9f30d65cd44172", src: src};                
        } else if ( /ca\.eonline\.com/.test( host ) ) {
            return { host : "ca.eonline.com", key : "cf23d8bd57050fbcb409fcbd24ba88b5", src: src};                
        } 

    }
    function isIE () {
	  var myNav = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
	  return (myNav.indexOf('msie') != -1) ? parseInt(myNav.split('msie')[1]) : false;
	}
    var enableIdx = true && (isIE() === false || isIE() > 9) && eol.page.context.locale.advertisements == 'us' && 'us' == 'us';
	if (enableIdx) {
	   	eolIdx.init(idxConfig);
   	}
	var enableAnonComment = false;
    var thymeConfig = { 
    		clientSite: 'www.eonline.com',//getThyme( window.location.host ).host,
    		contentID: '738819',
    		contentTypeID: 1,
    		labelLanguage: "us",
    		apiKey: getThyme( window.location.host ).key,
    		onCommentsChange: function(element){
   		    	if (typeof lp_global !== 'undefined'){
   		    		setTimeout("lp_global.AdjustLayout(true, false)", 500)  		    		
   		    	}   
   			},
			id:"thyme_comment",
			enableTheme:true,
			theme:"block",
			order:-1,
			anonComment:enableAnonComment,
			enableFacebook:true,
			enableTwitter:true,
			enableIDX:enableIdx,
			sizeOfList: 12,
			labels: {
				'en': { 
					addCommentHeading:'Leave a Comment', 
					addCommentButton:'Post Comment', 
					postComment:'Post Comment >', 
					sortBy:'', 
					newest:'Most Recent', 
					oldest: '', 
					rating:'Favorites', 
					reply:'Reply', 
					loadMoreComments:'See More Comments', 
					minuteAgo:'m', 
					minutesAgo:'m', 
					hourAgo:'h', 
					hoursAgo:'h',
					articleHas:'This article has'
				}
		    }
    	}; 
    
    
    function refreshThyme() {
    	tc = document.getElementById("thyme_comment");
    	if (tc != null) {
    		tc.innerHTML = '';
    	}
    	te = document.getElementById("thyme_script_block");
    	if (te != null) {
    		te.parentNode.removeChild(te);
    	}
    	initThyme();
    };
    
    function initThyme() {
        var e = document.createElement('script'); 
        e.type = 'text/javascript'; 
        e.async = true;
        e.src = getThyme( window.location.host ).src;
        e.id='thyme_script_block'
        if (document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0]){
            var s0 = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
            s0.parentNode.insertBefore(e,s0);
        } else if (document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0]){
            document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].appendChild(e);
        } else {
            document.getElementsByTagName('body')[0].appendChild(e);
        }   	
        setTimeout(function() {
	        var el = document.getElementsByClassName('thyme-comment-list')[0];
	        if (el && !el.hasChildNodes()) {
	            var emptyChild = document.createElement('li');
	            emptyChild.className = 'no-comment';
	            var textNode = document.createTextNode('Be the first to comment.');
	            emptyChild.appendChild(textNode);
				el.appendChild(emptyChild);
                if(typeof lp_global !== "undefined"){
                    lp_global.AdjustLayout(true, false);
                }
	        }
        }, 2000);
    };
        
    (function() {
    	initThyme()
    })();
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
	function ShowTab(TabID) {
		jQuery('.Footer_TabBlock_Tab').each(function (index) {
			if (jQuery(this).prop('id') == TabID) {
				jQuery(this).toggleClass('active');
			} else {
				jQuery(this).removeClass('active');
			}
		})
	};
	//Additional Privacy Statement pop up
	jQuery(".Newsletter_footer_aps").click(function(){
		//jQuery(this:hover).css("text-decoration","underline");
		jQuery("<div class='newsletter_aps_backdrop'></div>").appendTo(jQuery(document.body));

		jQuery(".newsletter_aps_backdrop").show();
		jQuery(".newsletter_aps_backdrop").fadeIn("slow");
		jQuery(".Newsletter_aps_box").show();
		var footerW = jQuery("#Footer_Layout").width();
		var apsL = (footerW - 291)/2;
		jQuery(".Newsletter_aps_box").css("margin-left", apsL+"px");
		isiPad = navigator.userAgent.match(/iPad/i) != null;
		if(isiPad){
			jQuery(".Newsletter_aps_box").css("height", "280px");
		}
		
		
	});
	jQuery(".newsletter_aps_backdrop, .Newsletter_aps_close, .Newsletter_aps_done_btn").live("click", function(){
		jQuery(".newsletter_aps_backdrop").remove();
		jQuery(".Newsletter_aps_box").hide();
		jQuery(".NavR_Newsletter_aps_box").hide();
	});
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
(function($){
	//set translated text and append confirmation overlays 
	setOverlayContent("Success! <br/> Thank you for subscribing.","","Success! <br/> Thank you for subscribing.","", "Close");
	appendOverlays("footer","us");
	
	jQuery(".Footer_TabBlock_Body #Newsletter_Submitting_Form input[name='footer_subscribe']").click(function(){
		HandleNewsletterSubscribe(".Footer_TabBlock_Tab");
	});
	
	//check footer custom check box
	jQuery(".Footer_TabBlock_Body #Newsletter_Submitting_Form .footer_custom_checkbox").toggle(function(){
			jQuery(this).addClass("checked");
			jQuery(".Footer_TabBlock_Body .newsletter_submitting_form input[name='footer_agreement_checkbox']").prop("checked", true);
		}, function(){
			jQuery(this).removeClass("checked");
			jQuery(".Footer_TabBlock_Body .newsletter_submitting_form input[name='footer_agreement_checkbox']").prop("checked", false);
	});
	
	//check header custom check box
	jQuery(".navr_newsletter #Newsletter_Submitting_Form .footer_custom_checkbox").toggle(function(){
			jQuery(this).addClass("checked");
			jQuery(".navr_newsletter .newsletter_submitting_form input[name='footer_agreement_checkbox']").prop("checked", true);
		}, function(){
			jQuery(this).removeClass("checked");
			jQuery(".navr_newsletter .newsletter_submitting_form input[name='footer_agreement_checkbox']").prop("checked", false);
	});
	
	//Closing the overlay
	jQuery(".footer_confirmation input, .footer_lightbox_close").click(function(){
		jQuery(".footer_confirmation_overlay").css({"display":"none"});
		jQuery(".footer_confirmation").css({"display":"none"});
		jQuery("#chkNewsletter_3").prop("checked", false);
		jQuery("#Newsletter_Email").val("Email Address");
		jQuery("#Newsletters .Newsletter_sending_animation").css({"display":"none"});
		jQuery("#Newsletters #Newsletter_Block").css({"display":"block"});
		jQuery("#Newsletter_Submitting_Form .footer_custom_checkbox").removeClass("checked");
	});
})(jQuery.noConflict());
function HandleNewsletterSubscribe(location) {
    var reqCheck = jQuery(location).find(".reqCheckBox").prop('checked');
    var email_val = jQuery(location).find("#Newsletter_Email").val();
    var isValidEmail = isEmail(email_val); 
           
	if(reqCheck && email_val != "" && isValidEmail){  
		jQuery(location).find(".mustSelect, .mustEnterEmail").hide();
		jQuery(location).find(".Newsletter_sending_animation").css({"display":"block"});
		jQuery(location).find("#Newsletter_Block").css({"display":"none"});
		// post: newsletterLookUp located in /resources/newsletter/js/newsletter.js 
		newsletterLookUp(email_val, "footerNewsletter", "us");
	}else{
		if (email_val == "" || !isValidEmail) {
			jQuery(location).find("#Newsletter_Email").focus();
			jQuery(location).find(".mustEnterEmail").show();
			}
		else {
			jQuery(location).find(".mustEnterEmail").hide();
		}
		if(!reqCheck){
			jQuery(location).find(".reqCheckBox").focus();
			jQuery(location).find(".mustSelect").show();
		}else{
			jQuery(location).find(".mustSelect").hide();
		}	
		return;
	}
};
</script>

	<!-- EOL: Loads the Standard Event (SE) function, which will only be used below when (isNielsenFound === false). -->
	<script type="text/javascript" src="/resources/js/libs/nielsen/adTracking.siteCensus.js"></script>

	<script id="no-search-block" type="text/javascript">
		/* EOL: Checks for the existence of the NBCUDigitalAdOps.com Nielsen injected code, 
		 * to determine if we need to initiate the Nielsen Standard Event tracking call or 
		 * if NBCUDigitalAdOps.com has already done it for us on the current page.
		 * This will avoid double counting, since we can't edit NBCUDigitalAdOps.com's code.
		 * Don't remove the id attribute from the script tag above. We want the isNielsenFound 
		 * search below to skip over the contents of this tag. Otherwise, it will try to match 
		 * the search key with what's in this script block.
		 */
		if ((typeof(eonline) !== 'undefined') && (typeof(eonline.nielsen) !== 'undefined')) {
			jQuery(document).ready(function($){
				/* EOL: JS will load the contents of this script block into memory. As we grab a copy of the body tag from the DOM,
				 * we have to wipe the DOM's "no-search-block" contents out, so that the indexOf (string search) function won't flag the search key as a match.
				 * The key to this coolness, is that the JS RAM "no-search-block" is still resident in memory & still executing!
				 * So these instructions aren't "deleted", but are still processed. Net Effect: A no-search-block has been created, that is contained inside of 
				 * the document.body tag, which can search for & detect a 3rd-party JS loaded -> JS loaded -> document.write('injected string');
				 */
				setTimeout(function() {
					var objNoSearchBlock = $("#no-search-block");
					objNoSearchBlock.html("");

					// EOL: Now using the code that's still in memory, we can run this search:
					var strDom = document.body.innerHTML;
					var isNielsenFound = ((strDom.indexOf('ci=us-505504h&cg=0&') > -1) || (strDom.indexOf('ci=us-505504h&amp;cg=0&amp;') > -1) || (strDom.indexOf('ci%3Dus-505504h%26cg%3D0%26') > -1));
					// Btw... We're looking for this: "ci=us-505504h&cg=0&" to make sure that we're not matching on "&cg=012345" or "&cg=event".

					// EOL: If not found, then makes the Nielsen SE blank pixel image tracking call:
					var useDebug = (location.href.indexOf('debug=Nielsen') > -1);
					if (!isNielsenFound) {
						if (typeof(eonline.nielsen.fbl) !== 'undefined') { 
							eonline.nielsen.fbl("NBCUDigitalAdOps.com's Nielsen Tracking Code Not Found - Calling Eonline.com's nielsenStandardEvent() function.", useDebug);
						}
						if (typeof(eonline.nielsen.standardEvent) !== 'undefined') { 
							eonline.nielsen.standardEvent('us', useDebug);
						}
					} else {
						if (typeof(eonline.nielsen.fbl) !== 'undefined') { 
							eonline.nielsen.fbl("NBCUDigitalAdOps.com's Nielsen Tracking Code Detected - Skipping Eonline.com's Nielsen SE call to avoid double counting.", useDebug);
						}
					}

					
					if (typeof(eraseCookie) !== 'undefined') {
						eraseCookie('useNielsenDebugger');
					}
					if (('news' === 'photos') && ('detail' === 'gallery') && (useDebug) && (typeof(createCookie) !== 'undefined')) {
						createCookie('useNielsenDebugger', useDebug, 1);
					}
				},500);
			});
		}
	</script>
